  //<![CDATA[
    function loadScript(url, callback) {
      var script = document.createElement("script");
      script.type = "text/javascript";
    
      if (script.readyState) {  //Internet Explorer
          script.onreadystatechange = function() {
            if (script.readyState == "loaded" ||
                    script.readyState == "complete") {
              script.onreadystatechange = null;
              callback();
            }
          };
      } else {  //Other browsers
        script.onload = function() {
          callback();
        };
      }
    
      script.src = url;
      document.getElementsByTagName("head")[0].appendChild(script);
    }
    
    function initAppleId() {
      AppleID.auth.init({
        clientId : 'com.goodreads.app', 
        scope : 'name email',
        redirectURI: 'https://www.goodreads.com/apple_users/sign_in_with_apple_web',
        state: 'apple_oauth_state_1a619156-9195-481c-9cbf-763ffaa36fbd'
      });
    }
    
    var initializeSiwa = function() {
      var APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL =  "https://appleid.cdn-apple.com/appleauth/static/jsapi/appleid/1/en_US/appleid.auth.js"
      loadScript(APPLE_SIGN_IN_JS_URL, initAppleId);
    };

      initAppleId();
    } else {
      initializeSiwa();
    }

      <div id="description" class="readable stacked" style="right:0">
        
<span id="freeTextContainer4604921504553760869">New York book editor Maris Matherly-Reed knows a best seller when she sees one - even if it is just a tantalizing partial manuscript submitted by a writer identified only as P.M.E., with the return address of an obscure island off the Georgia coast. Maris is intrigued enough to search for him.<br/><br/>Her trip to Georgia to meet the mysterious author takes her to an eerie, ruined c</span>
  <span id="freeText4604921504553760869" style="display:none">New York book editor Maris Matherly-Reed knows a best seller when she sees one - even if it is just a tantalizing partial manuscript submitted by a writer identified only as P.M.E., with the return address of an obscure island off the Georgia coast. Maris is intrigued enough to search for him.<br /><br />Her trip to Georgia to meet the mysterious author takes her to an eerie, ruined cotton plantation, where Maris finds Parker Evans, a man confined to a wheelchair who carefully hides his past. Coaxing his novel from him chaper by chapter, Maris becomes caught up in his tale of two friends who rent a boat with a young woman for a night of sex and drinking. Only one person will return from that trip.<br /><br />Disturbed about her sexual attraction to Parker and worried about her marriage to author and her co-publisher Noah Reed, Maris returns to New York, where the delivery of Parker's newest chapters convince her they are more than fiction. She wonders how well she knows her husband and begins a harrowing search for a truth that ties back to a terrifying crime and a man who will use her, or anyone, to get his revenge.<br /><br />©2001 Sandra Brown Management, Ltd; (P)2001 Simon &amp; Schuster Inc.; AUDIOWORKS Is an Imprint of Simon &amp; Schuster Audio Division, Simon &amp; Schuster Inc.</span>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1061765363" class="readable"

<span id="freeTextContainer7254868522245756364"><a href='http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/envycollage_zpsd7c9cd03.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412901446i/11439169.jpg' alt=' photo envycollage_zpsd7c9cd03.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>Envy was such a remarkable book. I have not read any other books by Sandra Brown so of course I didn't know what to expect. I read two amazing reviews and decided to give it a go.<br/><br/>When I started reading Envy, I could not put it down. It was that kind of book that I read every free moment I had. Finishing each chapter craving the next. I loved EVERYTHING about it. The characters, the location, the mystery. <br/><br/><a href='http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/7b27959564a0f7c8c2208790694fba7b_zps519c0971.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
  <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412901446i/11439170.jpg' alt=' photo 7b27959564a0f7c8c2208790694fba7b_zps519c0971.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
</a><br/><br/>For me, what made it so great was the depth of the characters and the mystery. It wa</span>
  <span id="freeText7254868522245756364" style="display:none"><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/envycollage_zpsd7c9cd03.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412901446i/11439169.jpg" alt=" photo envycollage_zpsd7c9cd03.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Envy was such a remarkable book. I have not read any other books by Sandra Brown so of course I didn't know what to expect. I read two amazing reviews and decided to give it a go.<br><br>When I started reading Envy, I could not put it down. It was that kind of book that I read every free moment I had. Finishing each chapter craving the next. I loved EVERYTHING about it. The characters, the location, the mystery. <br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/7b27959564a0f7c8c2208790694fba7b_zps519c0971.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412901446i/11439170.jpg" alt=" photo 7b27959564a0f7c8c2208790694fba7b_zps519c0971.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>For me, what made it so great was the depth of the characters and the mystery. It was also told in the present lives of the characters as well as in the past. There was no waiting for the mystery and intrigue. Right from the beginning it was as though Sandra Brown had opened Pandora’s Box. As a reader you are left needing to know the what, the who and the why.<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/145d7c1d-990d-4642-8b6f-2ef62be0c333_zps9871c786.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412901446i/11439171.jpg" alt=" photo 145d7c1d-990d-4642-8b6f-2ef62be0c333_zps9871c786.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>Sandra Brown’s writing style is incredible. The main characters were complex and amazing. There wasn’t anything simple about them. Even the side characters, Mike, Nadia and Daniel added more mystery and kept you guessing motives and connections.<br><br>Sandra Brown doesn't make things easy for the reader which made everything so captivating. There was no skimming in this book. Every word was important to read. The building of the plot, the suspense and the conundrum at the heart of this “story” was remarkable!<br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/fb7b6216-daee-4400-bba3-bbb1dd40dbf3_zps6b819cdb.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412129765i/11329100.jpg" alt=" photo fb7b6216-daee-4400-bba3-bbb1dd40dbf3_zps6b819cdb.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br>And finally, I am sure you know that I love my sexy reads and all things romance. While this book was different, filled with suspense, twists and turns, I still got my romance. I still got the passion I love. <br><br><a href="http://s797.photobucket.com/user/pramslar/media/a16ec2197410fb2fe9b187a22ae1c1c8_zpsf6a71c3b.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412901446i/11439172.jpg" alt=" photo a16ec2197410fb2fe9b187a22ae1c1c8_zpsf6a71c3b.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><i>"I'm not pretty, Maris." "You're beautiful." Tentatively, she leaned toward him. He didn't stop her. She began at his neck and kissed her way down. Her lips whisked across his skin, her tongue licked it softly. Her mouth wetly covered his nipple and he hissed a profanity and sank his fingers into her hair....</i><br><br>It has been said in other reviews that you should go into this book blind with no real background of the story and I couldn’t agree more. Yes, I read two review’s but they didn’t give anything away. Honestly, you shouldn’t have anything else floating around in your mind because you’re going to have to use every morsel of your head to absorb everything that goes on. :)<br><br><b>LOVED LOVED LOVED IT!</b> If you love Sandra Brown and haven’t read Envy, you <b>MUST</b> read it soon. If you have never read a book by Sandra Brown then I think Envy would be the perfect book for you!<br></span>
  <a data-text-id="7254868522245756364" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/781765915?book_show_action=true">Dec 05, 2013</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Mo" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Mo" href="/user/show/11856352-mo">Mo</a>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19437947-envy">review of another edition</a>


        

    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer781765915" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer17895132867423638016"><blockquote>
  <b> Living on a remote island under an assumed name, novelist Parker Evans guards his secrets well. Fascinated by this reclusive genius, publisher Maris Matherly-Reed decides to pursue him. But this new project threatens an old commitment, a commitment at the very center of her life.</b>
</blockquote><br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411136864ra/11196481.gif' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>There are plenty of twists and turns and some of them may be a bit predictable but they kept me on my toes.<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411136922i/11196488._SX540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>I really don’t want to say too much about the plot. You are better off just diving into the book.<br/><br/><blockquote>
  <b>“It take</b></blockquote></span>
  <span id="freeText17895132867423638016" style="display:none"><blockquote>
  <b> Living on a remote island under an assumed name, novelist Parker Evans guards his secrets well. Fascinated by this reclusive genius, publisher Maris Matherly-Reed decides to pursue him. But this new project threatens an old commitment, a commitment at the very center of her life.</b>
</blockquote><br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1411136864ra/11196481.gif" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There are plenty of twists and turns and some of them may be a bit predictable but they kept me on my toes.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411136922i/11196488._SX540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>I really don’t want to say too much about the plot. You are better off just diving into the book.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“It takes far less courage to cling to the past than it does to face the future".” </b>
</blockquote><br><br>It is like a story within a story, if that makes sense.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“He gathered a handful of her hair, then wound it around his fist and drew her closer until their faces were inches apart. He hesitated for several heartbeats, then settled his lips against hers, tested the angle, readjusted. He was moderately controlled until he heard a small whimper from her. He backed off, looked down into her eyes, and recognized a desire that equaled his own.<br>Control was abandoned. He covered her face with wild, random, artless kisses and she was doing the same to him. Then mouths melded and tongues touched, and they kissed with carnal greed.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br>The hero is an ass quite a bit of the time. I know that will be a plus for some of you. But he has his reasons.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411136864i/11196482._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>There is laughter, tears, mystery, love, hate, greed, sex … envy.<br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“Women readers aren`t turned on by nice heroes any more than male readers lust after heroines who are too virtuous.There should be at least a hint,maybe even a promise, of corruptibility.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411136864i/11196483.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><blockquote>
  <b>“The F word turns me on, she whispered. <br>"The F word?"<br>"Food"<br>He threw back his head and laughed. It rumbled up out of his chest and felt so good it startled him. For the first time in years,his laughter was spontaneous. It wasn`t tinged with bitterness and cynicism.” </b>
</blockquote><br><br>This is about the third or fourth Sandra Brown book that I have read and they have all been excellent.<br><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411136974i/11196501.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1411136864i/11196484._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></span>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/6972914-karen?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1059192783" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer2354548302764641510"><b>5 STARS ★★★★★<br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471380349i/20040759._SY540_.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/><br/>This book was SENSATIONAL!</b> In fact I don’t even know where to begin with this review. It is definitely the type of book that you should go into blind. Don’t read any descriptions or possible spoilers… just read the book. I will not describe the story here… it is unnecessary to do so. You are much better off in your own head with this, trust me.<br/><br/>What I will say is that it totally caught me off-guard. This was the first book I’ve read by Sandra Brown, and it will definitely NOT BE THE </span>
  <span id="freeText2354548302764641510" style="display:none"><b>5 STARS ★★★★★<br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1471380349i/20040759._SY540_.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>This book was SENSATIONAL!</b> In fact I don’t even know where to begin with this review. It is definitely the type of book that you should go into blind. Don’t read any descriptions or possible spoilers… just read the book. I will not describe the story here… it is unnecessary to do so. You are much better off in your own head with this, trust me.<br><br>What I will say is that it totally caught me off-guard. This was the first book I’ve read by Sandra Brown, and it will definitely NOT BE THE LAST. She is a fantastic writer. Her writing style, her description, her characters… oh my God… these characters were so incredibly rich and juicy…so dark and complex. I fucking LOVED being in their heads. The story is told from multiple points of view, providing some really interesting insight into their motivations. And the plot was brilliantly laid out. Edge-of-your-seat kind of stuff…from start to finish. Just brilliant.<br><br>It will blow your freaking mind!!!! <br><br>And just in case you were wondering… is it a romance? It most definitely is, in the purest sense of the word. But you will have to work hard for it. You may have to bleed for it. But it’s there, behind all the trap doors and heavy curtains. And it is beautiful.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/52f2389c274d8d6131ed783a9af0af79.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412006506i/11310576._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 52f2389c274d8d6131ed783a9af0af79.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i>Writing was demanding, solitary, backbreaking work. A writer mined the tunnels of his brain, using words for his pickaxe. A week’s effort might yield only one nugget that was worth keeping, and you could weep with pathetic gratitude over that.</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Couples/e27abee4aade42bfd892bccb0c1ca2cd.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412006506i/11310577.jpg" alt=" photo e27abee4aade42bfd892bccb0c1ca2cd.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> “Control was abandoned. He covered her face with wild, random, artless kisses and she was doing the same to him. Then mouths melded and tongues touched, and they kissed with carnal greed.”</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Objects/575b1ba33ed510d79937f82af9f95398.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412006506i/11310578._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 575b1ba33ed510d79937f82af9f95398.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><br><b>
  <i> ‘Some human characteristics are common to us all. Manifestation of these characteristics is dependent upon circumstance. Everyone has temporary displays of fear, happiness, frustration and so on.’<br><br> ‘Other traits are unique to certain individuals. They define the person and his character. Among these traits are admirable examples like humility, charity, bravery.’<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/24c30abecea1bafabc08f6a63e562482.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412006506i/11310579._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 24c30abecea1bafabc08f6a63e562482.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><b>Parker</b><br><br> ‘Unfortunately these have dark counterparts like jealousy, greed, and envy. Persons governed by one of these traits typically cloak it with charm, and most are very successful at it, because along with the trait invariably comes the cunning to conceal it.’<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Men/7b8acddb7a5e6768ccdd58a98409f0a2.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1410999147i/11181403._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 7b8acddb7a5e6768ccdd58a98409f0a2.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a><br><b>Noah</b><br><br> ‘Nevertheless, the trait lives and matures inside them as insidiously as an eel inside a cave, waiting, even anticipating, the times with it can strike anything or anyone that threatens.’</i>
</b><br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Women/1e265bf37b0ea85a982cab9c1ce252db.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
  <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1412006506i/11310580._SY540_.jpg" alt=" photo 1e265bf37b0ea85a982cab9c1ce252db.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
</a><br><b>Maris</b><br><br>I have no more to add. You will love this.<br><br><span>[image error]</span><a href="http://s1253.photobucket.com/user/kgourgues/media/Tags/e15e849879b26529fb2c4c95fb266233.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">

<div id="review_1081417131" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1081417131" />
    <a title="Ingie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie"><img alt="Ingie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1477339772p2/15589375.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1081417131?book_show_action=true">Oct 16, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Ingie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Ingie" href="/user/show/15589375-ingie">Ingie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audible Audio " href="/book/show/13599369-envy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-audio">romance-m-f-audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=books-i-read-2015">books-i-read-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=c-amazing-5-stars-2015">c-amazing-5-stars-2015</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=romance-m-f-suspense">romance-m-f-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/15589375-ingie?shelf=novel-thriller-crime-fiction">novel-thriller-crime-fiction</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1081417131" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer41907159839655654"><i>Written March 15, 2015</i><br/><br/><b>4.7 Stars - Top quality crime novel with a nice romance touch. Add a superb narrator making it so very exciting</b><br/><br/>At last was it time for a <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown' title='Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sandra Brown</a> book. My friends Karen and Mo's so beloved suspense / crime writer. I crossed my fingers for a great start to a new author with has a high pile of beloved books to choose from.<br/><blockquote>
  <a href='http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/image.jpg2_zpsppczicja.jpg.html' target='_blank' rel='nofollow noopener'>
    <img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426355141i/14005392.jpg' alt=' photo image.jpg2_zpsppczicja.jpg' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/>
  </a>
</blockquote><br/><b>High Five! ~ For a new book-life with <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown' title='Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sandra Brown</a></b><br/>This was a great novel, with a thrilling good crime plot and a sweet romance part. I loved</span>
  <span id="freeText41907159839655654" style="display:none"><i>Written March 15, 2015</i><br><br><b>4.7 Stars - Top quality crime novel with a nice romance touch. Add a superb narrator making it so very exciting</b><br><br>At last was it time for a <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown" title="Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Sandra Brown</a> book. My friends Karen and Mo's so beloved suspense / crime writer. I crossed my fingers for a great start to a new author with has a high pile of beloved books to choose from.<br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/Stars/image.jpg2_zpsppczicja.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426355141i/14005392.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg2_zpsppczicja.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
</blockquote><br><b>High Five! ~ For a new book-life with <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown" title="Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Sandra Brown</a></b><br>This was a great novel, with a thrilling good crime plot and a sweet romance part. I loved it all and I was kind if exhausted and drained after over 14 exciting audiobooks hours. — I needed a night to summarize my thoughts.<br><br>***********************************************************<br><blockquote>
  <b>“It takes far less courage to cling to the past than it does to face the future.”</b>
</blockquote><br><i>New York and Georgia 2002</i><br><br>Something horrible happened three summer happy 'youngsters' on a boat trip 1988. The (shy and hiding) novelist <b>Parker Evans</b>, living on a, once grand but nowadays ruined, cotton plantation on a small <i>Georgia</i> island, tells us a sad story about two college kids and an unsolved death. <br><blockquote>
  <a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/City%20and%20nature%20etc/Sea/image.jpg2_zpsw6q10y7o.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener">
    <img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426177082i/13984736.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg2_zpsw6q10y7o.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg">
  </a>
  <b></b>
</blockquote><br><i>Envy</i> is also the story about the <i>New York</i> book editor (publisher) <b>Maris Matherly-Reed </b> who feels an interest in a tantalizing partial manuscript submitted by a writer identified only as P.M.E. <br><br>Maris has a goodlooking former rake and womanizer, the talanted (one success novel) author and co-publisher <b>Noah Reed</b>, as her husband. But things has started to feel odd and Maris starts to wondering if she really know her husband? Is there something wrong or are she just imagine it all? <br><br>***********************************************************<br><br><b>The audiobook edition, narrator etc</b><br>I listened to the 14:40 hrs audiobook narrated by <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/1330869.Victor_Slezak" title="Victor Slezak" rel="nofollow noopener">Victor Slezak</a>. He was simply fantastic. Not a tiny little complaining from me. Not one bad character voice or any lacks whatsoever. I have a fondness for male deep voiced narrators and here I got another favorite to that bunch. ~ I'll for sure search for more books read by him. <br><br>***********************************************************<br><br><b><i>Envy</i> is a story about old debilitating ugly envy (course) and a book in the book</b>, but also a novel about our love for books, the struggle with writing and those who tells a really good story. As this story. <br><blockquote>“Women readers aren't turned on by nice heroes any more than male readers lust after heroines who are too virtuous. There should be at least a hint, maybe even a promise, of corruptibility.” <br><br><a href="http://s1332.photobucket.com/user/Li64/media/City%20and%20nature%20etc/Place/image.jpg2_zpsf8qfztue.jpg.html" target="_blank" rel="nofollow noopener"><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1426193995i/13986465.jpg" alt=" photo image.jpg2_zpsf8qfztue.jpg" class="gr-hostedUserImg"></a>
</blockquote><br>I'm not sure this should be labeled as just a crime romance. I should recommend it to all novel readers in the bigger fiction crime genre. Even hubbies, brothers or non romances loving girlfriends. This is romantic, and sexy enough, but that's more a second (wonderful) topic, which I liked. <br><br>***********************************************************<br><br><b>I may have guessed some</b> of the outcomes in the (very well done) plot quite early, but I don't want spoil anymore here, so I stay with these words. ~ Highly recommended! I just found a new favorite author to enjoy in the future. I like clever stories...good brain training. <br><br><b>I LIKE - yep, enormously glad about it</b></span>
  <a data-text-id="41907159839655654" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

<div id="review_1532285564" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1532285564" />
    <a title="Jennifer" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer"><img alt="Jennifer" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1394406877p2/2473504.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1532285564?book_show_action=true">Jan 31, 2016</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jennifer" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jennifer" href="/user/show/2473504-jennifer">Jennifer</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19437947-envy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=adult-content">adult-content</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=i-met-the-author">i-met-the-author</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=listened-to-audiobook">listened-to-audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=stand-alone-novel">stand-alone-novel</a>,

              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/2473504-jennifer?shelf=read-2016">read-2016</a>
          </div>

        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1532285564" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15956580280966636616"><a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/76179.Envy' title='Envy by Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Envy</a> is a standalone, thriller/mystery novel written by author <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown' title='Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Sandra Brown</a>. I just discovered Ms. Brown in 2014 and obviously haven't read <b>all</b> of her novels yet, but based on what I have read I had already come to my own conclusion that her recent novels are bounds better than anything she has written in the past.<br/><br/><img src='https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454635814ra/17993995.gif' width='400' height='220' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/><br/>Yeah...I was wrong. Not that her new stuff isn't good! OMG, <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20454672.Mean_Streak' title='Mean Streak by Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Mean Streak</a> and <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25114548.Friction' title='Friction by Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Friction</a> are freakin' amazing! But <a href='https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/76179.Envy' title='Envy by Sandra Brown' rel='nofollow noopener'>Envy</a> is just as good, and fortunately for me, my premature conclusion has</span>
  <span id="freeText15956580280966636616" style="display:none"><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/76179.Envy" title="Envy by Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Envy</a> is a standalone, thriller/mystery novel written by author <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown" title="Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Sandra Brown</a>. I just discovered Ms. Brown in 2014 and obviously haven't read <b>all</b> of her novels yet, but based on what I have read I had already come to my own conclusion that her recent novels are bounds better than anything she has written in the past.<br><br><img src="https://images.gr-assets.com/hostedimages/1454635814ra/17993995.gif" width="400" height="220" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Yeah...I was wrong. Not that her new stuff isn't good! OMG, <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/20454672.Mean_Streak" title="Mean Streak by Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Mean Streak</a> and <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/25114548.Friction" title="Friction by Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Friction</a> are freakin' amazing! But <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/76179.Envy" title="Envy by Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Envy</a> is just as good, and fortunately for me, my premature conclusion has just been dismissed.<br><br><a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/76179.Envy" title="Envy by Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Envy</a> features an array of mysteriously complicated relationships, it shows the ugliness of envy, deceit, and revenge, and it's a book about writing a book for God's sake! Oh...I forgot to mention one tiny, little thing: wheelchair sex. Let's just say that although our hero may have some physical limitations, his virility is not one of them. Mmmmm.<br><br>I'm glad I gave <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/book/show/76179.Envy" title="Envy by Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Envy</a> a chance even though I <i>thought</i> I had already read the author's best work. I've opened myself up to an entire library of <a href="https://www.goodreads.com/author/show/6218.Sandra_Brown" title="Sandra Brown" rel="nofollow noopener">Sandra Brown</a> thrillers and I'm super excited! Check her out!<br><br><b>My favorite quote:</b><br><i>"Everyone is opportunistic. Everyone. Without exception. Only the degree of one's opportunism separates him from others. How far is one willing to go to get what he wants?"</i><br><br><br><b>01/31/16:</b><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1454294077i/17941251.jpg" width="400" height="340" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br>Review to come...</span>

<div id="review_27855004" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/27855004" />
    <a title="Tammy" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/785960-tammy"><img alt="Tammy" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1553824694p2/785960.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/27855004?book_show_action=true">Jul 21, 2008</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Tammy" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Tammy" href="/user/show/785960-tammy">Tammy</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>


          <div><span class="uitext greyText">Recommends it for: </span>
           <span class="uitext reviewText">fans of intense mysteries</span></div>

          <div>
    <span class="greyText">Recommended to Tammy by: </span>
      Terhan
  </div>


          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/785960-tammy?shelf=2008-reads">2008-reads</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/785960-tammy?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer27855004" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer12561137510163071116">Who knew Sandra Brown could write sexy and scary so well together? <br/><br/>My neighbor did, I suppose. She has been pushing this book off on me for the past year and I finally gave in and read it over the holiday. So glad I did!<br/><br/>New York publisher, Maris "Matherly" Reed, receives an intriguing manuscript regarding two college kids and an unsolved murder from someone identified only as P.M.E. She feels compelled to meet the anonymous author, so she travels to a remote Georgia island and begins snooping ar</span>
  <span id="freeText12561137510163071116" style="display:none">Who knew Sandra Brown could write sexy and scary so well together? <br /><br />My neighbor did, I suppose. She has been pushing this book off on me for the past year and I finally gave in and read it over the holiday. So glad I did!<br /><br />New York publisher, Maris "Matherly" Reed, receives an intriguing manuscript regarding two college kids and an unsolved murder from someone identified only as P.M.E. She feels compelled to meet the anonymous author, so she travels to a remote Georgia island and begins snooping around. On a cotton plantation she finds razor sharp Parker Evens, a man who is concealing his true identity and his ties to Maris. <br /><br />There were several subplots and twists to this story that kept me on the edge of my seat, including an interesting subplot with Maris's sleezy husband, Noah, and her nemesis, Nadia. Like I said - this one is a real nailbiter. I am off to get a manicure now. =) </span>
  <a data-text-id="12561137510163071116" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1208962938" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1208962938" />
    <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/27276528-liz"><img alt="✰ Liz ✰ " src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1451097545p2/27276528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1208962938?book_show_action=true">Feb 22, 2015</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="✰ Liz ✰ " class="user" itemprop="url" name="✰ Liz ✰ " href="/user/show/27276528-liz">✰ Liz ✰ </a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>



        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=action-packed">action-packed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=healing">healing</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=abused">abused</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/27276528-liz?shelf=high-angst-alert">high-angst-alert</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1208962938" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer9402653472630246376"><b>“Envy. That’s what this is all about. Envy." </b><br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425009207i/13830252._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Sandra Brown is one of those authors that I have been wanting to check out for a long time. I see rave reviews of her work on my friends updates and walls. Her books have been sitting on my TBR shelf forever! I simply cannot rave enough about my first Sandra Brown read! Envy has suspense, a well developed plot, intriguing characters, greed, romance, and of course envy!<br/><br/><img src='https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425009207i/13830253._SY540_.jpg' width='400' height='400' alt='description' class='gr-hostedUserImg'/> <br/><br/>Maris is a smart and savvy business woman. She is passionate about her job as an e</span>
  <span id="freeText9402653472630246376" style="display:none"><b>“Envy. That’s what this is all about. Envy." </b><br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425009207i/13830252._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Sandra Brown is one of those authors that I have been wanting to check out for a long time. I see rave reviews of her work on my friends updates and walls. Her books have been sitting on my TBR shelf forever! I simply cannot rave enough about my first Sandra Brown read! Envy has suspense, a well developed plot, intriguing characters, greed, romance, and of course envy!<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425009207i/13830253._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"> <br><br>Maris is a smart and savvy business woman. She is passionate about her job as an editor and has an amazing relationship with her father. <br><br> <b>"Her mother’s death could have been a heartache that wedged them apart. Instead, it had forged the bond between father and daughter. His discipline had been firm and consistent, but only rarely necessary." </b><br><br>I absolutely adored Daniel (Maris' father). He was such a kindred spirit. Oh the gift of a good parent is like nothing else in the world. I found myself rereading his dialogue as if it were a message from my own father.<br><br> <b>"Marriages go through periods like this. Even good marriages. Dry spells, if you will.”-Daniel </b><br><br>Professionally Maris is happy but personally she is struggling. Although she is married to a sophisticated equally savvy man, she knows that something is amiss. While immersed in her work, she comes across a prologue to a book entitled Envy. She makes her mind up to meet the author and enrage him to complete the book so that she can publish it. <br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425009207i/13830254._SY540_.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>Parker is the mysterious author of Envy. He has quite a story to tell. He is not a happy man. It took me a while to understand his character. It is the anticipation of knowing his past that keeps the reader engaged in the present story. <br><br>Maris leaves the hustle and bustle of the big city to visit Parker. She wants to pursue his book. She has no idea what she is walking in on. He is crass and gritty and full of spite. Maris is one hot headed heroine. When she has made up her mind, she won't stop until she gets exactly what she is after. <br><br>Maris thrives on the quiet island. She spends time listening to Parker read his novel. As the story is revealed, Maris becomes more comfortable with Parker. <br><br><b>"If he’d been forced to use an applicable adverb to describe the way in which they were looking at one another, he would choose “expectantly,” a modifier that combined curiosity with caution, wonderment with undertones of wariness."-Parker</b><br><br>Meanwhile, Noah (Maris' husband) is up to no good. As the plot slowly reveals itself, we see what kind of man Noah truly is.<br><br>Maris is such a great heroine. I loved watching her grow. She knows that she is doubting her marriage. She knows that she is feeling something for Parker and yet she cannot quite explain it.<br><br><b>“He’s the most complex individual I’ve ever met,”-Maris</b><br><br>Envy isn't just a love story (although the love story is a beautiful one). Envy is full of suspense, drama, failed friendships, and choices.<br><br><img src="https://i.gr-assets.com/images/S/compressed.photo.goodreads.com/hostedimages/1425009828i/13830301.jpg" width="400" height="400" alt="description" class="gr-hostedUserImg"><br><br>As much as I would love to give you more information about this story, I can't! I don't want to ruin it for you. It doesn't take long to put some of the pieces of the puzzle together and yet the full picture doesn't fall into place until the last few pages of the book. The pacing in Envy is perfect. About half way through the book, I simply could not put it down. I will not hesitate to read another Sandra Brown novel. Her writing is like dining in a 5 star restaurant. It's hard to hit the drive thru after experiencing such genius! <br><br> <b>"Maris had been essential to his plot, but he hadn’t expected her to become essential to him. In the brief time she had been in his life, she had become the most important element of it."-Parker</b><br> </span>
  <a data-text-id="9402653472630246376" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_1064674268" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1064674268" />
    <a title="Glass" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4808910-glass"><img alt="Glass" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1583244629p2/4808910.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1064674268?book_show_action=true">Sep 26, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Glass" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Glass" href="/user/show/4808910-glass">Glass</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19437947-envy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=fangirling-like-crazy">fangirling-like-crazy</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=romance">romance</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4808910-glass?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1064674268" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer3501526782660722234"> This summer I started to read suspense/thriller novels and they became my new obsession. Yes, there are cliches even here, but nothing that I can't get over. I thought that there would be no one better than Linda Howard. And then I started to read Sandra Brown.<br/><br/><b>Five reasons why you should read Envy:</b><br/><br/> <b>1.</b> Story that will keep your attention until the very end. It just pulls you in from the page one and doesn't let you go. I couldn't do anything else but read because I had to know what happens next.</span>
  <span id="freeText3501526782660722234" style="display:none"> This summer I started to read suspense/thriller novels and they became my new obsession. Yes, there are cliches even here, but nothing that I can't get over. I thought that there would be no one better than Linda Howard. And then I started to read Sandra Brown.<br /><br /><b>Five reasons why you should read Envy:</b><br /><br /> <b>1.</b> Story that will keep your attention until the very end. It just pulls you in from the page one and doesn't let you go. I couldn't do anything else but read because I had to know what happens next. And you get two stories in one - I should probably stop talking now before I spoil it for you. The best way to read this book would be just to pic it up an read. Don't ask too many questions.<br /><br /> <b>2.</b> Characters. So complex and well developed. You live and breathe with them.<br /><br /> <b>3.</b> Writing. And all parts about being a writer. I like to say that you can always notice when author writes about something that is familiar and personal for her/him, and there is nothing more personal for author than the very process of writing and creating fictional world.<br /> <br /> <b>4.</b> Angst, but not the kind of angst you will find in popular trashy romance novels. <br /><br /> <b>5.</b> Parker. He is heart and soul of this book and one of the most intriguing characters I've read about.<br /><br /><br /> But unfortunately, Envy didn't stay amazing all way trough. Last few chapters were rushed and filled with too much melodrama. I wish it ended differently, but still it was a good book.<br /><br /> <b>Who should read it?</b> Fans of good suspense stories. </span>
  <a data-text-id="3501526782660722234" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_1061443837" class="review nosyndicate" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/1061443837" />
    <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel"><img alt="♥Rachel♥" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1363996055p2/5481477.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/1061443837?book_show_action=true">Sep 22, 2014</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="♥Rachel♥" class="user" itemprop="url" name="♥Rachel♥" href="/user/show/5481477-rachel">♥Rachel♥</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Kindle Edition " href="/book/show/19437947-envy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=audio-book">audio-book</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=favorites">favorites</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/5481477-rachel?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer1061443837" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer6291442358776876431">To all outward appearances Maris Matherly-Reed leads a charmed life and has everything. Books have been her passion every since she can remember, and she’s the sole heir to the well respected Matherly Publishing. She’s totally immersed in the literary world and has a lot of power. Maris also snagged publishing’s most eligible bachelor, Noah Reed, the author of her favorite book. She was halfway in love with him even before laying eyes on him just because of his words. But seeing how gorgeous and</span>
  <span id="freeText6291442358776876431" style="display:none">To all outward appearances Maris Matherly-Reed leads a charmed life and has everything. Books have been her passion every since she can remember, and she’s the sole heir to the well respected Matherly Publishing. She’s totally immersed in the literary world and has a lot of power. Maris also snagged publishing’s most eligible bachelor, Noah Reed, the author of her favorite book. She was halfway in love with him even before laying eyes on him just because of his words. But seeing how gorgeous and charismatic he was, and the fact that he wanted <i>her </i>after breaking so many hearts was the icing on the cake. While marrying Noah seemed like a dream come true, things seem a little off to her now. <br /><br />Her doubts in regards to Noah get put on the back burner when a story from the “slush” pile catches Maris’ eye. She reads it and is hooked, but realizes the rest of the book is not there. Neither is the writer’s contact info, only the initials: P.M.E. <i>Envy</i>, as the prologue is called, recounts a day of celebration that goes horribly wrong and Maris desperately wants to know what happened. She feels compelled to search for the mysterious P.M.E. not knowing the secrets and past she’s about to uncover. <br /><b><br />Envy </b>was a real page turner with twists and connections at every corner. The villain was a master plotter, evil to the core; a narcissistic creep! After getting away with so much this person overestimated their cleverness and underestimated the intelligence of others; “pride comes before a fall” and I was eagerly looking forward to that fulfillment! It was sweet watching him/her get some of their own medicine because most of the book I wanted to reach into the pages and smack this person silly! <br /><br />I adored Maris! She was sweet, pure-hearted and looked for the best in people or a situation, but wasn’t stupid enough to fall for bullshit when someone is trying to spoon feed it to her. <br /><br />Our hero was unrefined and crass; a dirty talker who liked to shock, but one who had a vulnerable soft heart. He had an intense pull on Maris, and she affects him far more than he expected. Add in the steamy, sultry southern setting, and you have a recipe for a smoldering romance. <br /><b><br />Envy</b> was another score for Sandra Brown, and as usual with her books I was glued to the pages! I usually end up putting aside everything else so I can finish and find out how it all turns out. I think one of the best features of a Sandra Brown story is the fact that the bad guy usually gets a much deserved payback, one that is cleverly delivered. <b>Envy</b> was no exception and I was grinning in satisfaction when this villain got their comeuppance! If you love mysteries with a hot romance or romantic suspense and haven’t picked up a Sandra Brown novel, you are definitely missing out.<br /><br />This review is also posted at <a href="http://thereadersden.blogspot.com/2015/04/envy-by-sandra-brown.html" rel="nofollow noopener">The Readers Den.</a><br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="6291442358776876431" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<span id="freeTextContainer6248080734823868165">This is my favorite SB yet! Filled with mystery, intrigue, incredible suspense, unfathomable events and a heavy dose of sensual romance, I loved it. SB has a way of building things up, revealing little by little...making you think one thing while suspicious of another. And she does this all seamlessly and brilliantly. My mind is always working overtime when I read her work so it's no surprise I figured things out early on. It's not my keen mind but the knowledge that anything she writes has to b</span>
  <span id="freeText6248080734823868165" style="display:none">This is my favorite SB yet! Filled with mystery, intrigue, incredible suspense, unfathomable events and a heavy dose of sensual romance, I loved it. SB has a way of building things up, revealing little by little...making you think one thing while suspicious of another. And she does this all seamlessly and brilliantly. My mind is always working overtime when I read her work so it's no surprise I figured things out early on. It's not my keen mind but the knowledge that anything she writes has to be looked at in the most cunning of ways. Never take anything at face value and always suspect everyone, hence clueing into what happened. <br />Even suspecting things didn't prepare me for my reaction to how everything went down as portrayed in the prologue, it was heartbreakingly sinister. But seriously, writing a book about a writer writing his own book? That may sound redundant but it was done so well, so detailed I was blown away. I loved Maris and how she never gave up on Parker. The love scenes were trademark SB: erotic and sensual without being overly drawn out. I love that! It doesn't take from the story but adds that lovely romantic element I crave. <br /><br />And the way she describes things from the scenery to a characters action is flawless. I felt like I was in Georgia, I felt the claustrophobic humidity and smelled the foliage, just loved this and highly recommend it!<br /><br />Thanks Mo! &lt;3</span>

<div id="review_127303043" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/127303043" />
    <a title="Carrie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/1478411-carrie"><img alt="Carrie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1352063544p2/1478411.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/127303043?book_show_action=true">Oct 21, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Carrie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Carrie" href="/user/show/1478411-carrie">Carrie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Audiobook 9780743567763" href="/book/show/10132820-envy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=audio">audio</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=manipulative-friends-family">manipulative-friends-family</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=own">own</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=contemporary">contemporary</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=read-2012">read-2012</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=mystery">mystery</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=suspense">suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=read-2020">read-2020</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=re-read">re-read</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/1478411-carrie?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer127303043" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer10246214374303807298">6/30/20 I listened to this again and it was just as enjoyable.<br/><br/>Reviewed for Audiogals.net<br/><br/>Narrated by Viktor Slezak<br/><br/>Envy came to my attention over a year ago, but I kept putting it off because I feared it wouldn’t have enough relationship development. For decades I’d read straight mystery and suspense, and while I still love suspense, I now want books with a strong romantic element. Surely, I thought, Sandra Brown is too mainstream for my current tastes. How wrong I was, and how glad I am that I fi</span>
  <span id="freeText10246214374303807298" style="display:none">6/30/20 I listened to this again and it was just as enjoyable.<br /><br />Reviewed for Audiogals.net<br /><br />Narrated by Viktor Slezak<br /><br />Envy came to my attention over a year ago, but I kept putting it off because I feared it wouldn’t have enough relationship development. For decades I’d read straight mystery and suspense, and while I still love suspense, I now want books with a strong romantic element. Surely, I thought, Sandra Brown is too mainstream for my current tastes. How wrong I was, and how glad I am that I finally gave into the curiosity and bought the audiobook. If I'd read Envy in print I would have still give it an A. But, if you will excuse me for being effusive for a moment, Victor Slezak's narration is so perfect it makes me want to stop strangers on the street and force them to listen. <br />Envy is an amazingly well-crafted suspense story with a multilayer plot and perfect pacing. Sandra Brown immerses the listener in her story. Whether it's a big city, a college frat house, Key West, or an obscure Georgia island, the settings feel as important as any character in the book. This amazing ability to evoke a sense of place for her readers is one of the things I enjoy most about Brown’s writing. But the shining star in Envy is Brown’s incredibly well written suspense. The book consists of two story arcs that eventually intersect. One story arc starts when Maris, a publisher, receives the first chapter of a book in the mail. That manuscript peaks her interest, and sends Maris to an isolated island off the coast of Georgia in search of the reclusive author. Parker Evans is the author who submits the unsolicited manuscript to Maris’s publishing house. The second arc is the book Parker is writing, titled "Envy." The two story arcs are interwoven seamlessly, with Brown doling out the backstory contained in the manuscript in tantalizing installments. <br />In addition to the mystery in Parker's book, there is intrigue and betrayal going on in the present day story of Parker, Maris, Maris's husband (Noah), and her father. Brown alternates the present day story of Parker, Maris, Noah and the rest with chapters from Parker’s manuscript,” Envy.” I can’t emphasize enough how masterfully she builds the suspense story throughout this book. Both story arcs are full of enough detail to stand on their own, but when brought together, the result feels like much more than a sum of the parts.<br />While there are many important and well-developed characters in Envy, the relationship between Parker and Maris stands at the center of the book. Their uneasy, yet magnetic, partnership is the spark that sets off the present day chain of events, but it’s also what allows for healing in the end. Parker Evans is not a likeable man for much of the book, and it’s obvious he’s playing some deeper game than simply trying to get a book published. Maris tries to convince herself it’s only the book she’s interested in, but she’s soon questioning Parker’s motives as well as her own. Is she continuing to pursue the matter because of the manuscript or does the recalcitrant author have something to do with her continued visits to the island?<br />Victor Slezak voices all the characters well, but he has a special knack for the southern accents of Parker and his assistant, Mike. Slezak's voice for the often cantankerous Parker is deep, rough, and perfect. Slazek doesn't use a high voice for the female characters, but instead he softens his voice. All the voices are easy to differentiate and keeping track of who is speaking in a conversation is never a problem, even though there are many characters in this book. I honestly cannot think of any way to improve on the narration for this book.</span>
  <a data-text-id="10246214374303807298" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>

<div id="review_150406283" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/150406283" />
    <a title="Jamie" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/4605519-jamie"><img alt="Jamie" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1319681755p2/4605519.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/150406283?book_show_action=true">Feb 24, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jamie" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jamie" href="/user/show/4605519-jamie">Jamie</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="really liked it"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">really liked it</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p0"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780446527132" href="/book/show/537400.Envy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4605519-jamie?shelf=mystery-thriller">mystery-thriller</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/4605519-jamie?shelf=romance">romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer150406283" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer15459012382693719509">A great story by Sandra Brown. A near-perfect blend of romance, mystery and even suspense. The book has three focused characters. Maris, daughter of the CEO of a publishing company and editor. She is sent a prologue to a story that immediately captivates her. After some searching, she comes across the writer. The author is Parker, a bitter recluse. due to a horrid incident in his past, he was left in a wheelchair. The other main character is Noah, Maris' husband. Noah has a darker agenda to sell</span>
  <span id="freeText15459012382693719509" style="display:none">A great story by Sandra Brown. A near-perfect blend of romance, mystery and even suspense. The book has three focused characters. Maris, daughter of the CEO of a publishing company and editor. She is sent a prologue to a story that immediately captivates her. After some searching, she comes across the writer. The author is Parker, a bitter recluse. due to a horrid incident in his past, he was left in a wheelchair. The other main character is Noah, Maris' husband. Noah has a darker agenda to sell of the publishing company and make a hefty profit. This novel also closely follows the story Parker is writing and its characters. Soon Maris is questioning how much of this story is based on real life. Little does Maris know that Parker has his own agenda to fulfill.<br />This novel was nicely written, the characters were easy to love (or hate as the case may be). Some nice surprises ant twists throughout the book, following well into to suspense line. The romantic aspects were well blended into the story. A few things were a bit predicable but not overly so that you lose interest. The intrigue holds through to the very end. 4.5 stars<br />When I first read this, I vaguely remember that I loved it. Going back as an audiobook, I hated the narration. Unfortunately this cost the book my rounded up star. Way too monotone. Granted it was short, but it was just lacking in this format. So I recommend reading this for yourself.</span>
  <a data-text-id="15459012382693719509" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_241983714" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/241983714" />
    <a title="D.G." class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/210123-d-g"><img alt="D.G." src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1330353755p2/210123.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/241983714?book_show_action=true">Dec 01, 2011</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="D.G." class="user" itemprop="url" name="D.G." href="/user/show/210123-d-g">D.G.</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Hardcover 9780446527132" href="/book/show/537400.Envy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=audiobook">audiobook</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=reviewed">reviewed</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/210123-d-g?shelf=awesome-narration">awesome-narration</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer241983714" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer1554779675138911874">**4.5 stars**<br/><br/>This is a terrific romantic suspense book with one of the most despicable villains I've ever had the misfortune to find in fiction. There were tons of good twists and at times I was truly afraid that the villain would get away with murder but just when you thought everybody was well and truly f*cked, something would happen that would put the villain in his place. <br/><br/>I won't go into detail about the plot or characters because for the first couple of chapters the reader doesn't know who'</span>
  <span id="freeText1554779675138911874" style="display:none">**4.5 stars**<br /><br />This is a terrific romantic suspense book with one of the most despicable villains I've ever had the misfortune to find in fiction. There were tons of good twists and at times I was truly afraid that the villain would get away with murder but just when you thought everybody was well and truly f*cked, something would happen that would put the villain in his place. <br /><br />I won't go into detail about the plot or characters because for the first couple of chapters the reader doesn't know who's the villain and who's the hero (you can find out if you hunt around for a description but I liked not knowing for sure.) As usual with Sandra Brown, there are several POVs, intertwined with the chapters of "Envy" a book the heroine is editing (sort of a book within a book.) The author skillfully ties the narrative in this book so it gives you hints of the overall arc without revealing everything upfront. As somebody who is not familiar with the book writing process, I found all the discussions about writing, editing and publishing very interesting and I felt they didn't detract at all from the plot, but on the contrary, they gave you a hint about several important twists in the book.<br /><br />This book doesn't get 5 stars because I thought we needed an epilogue, mostly to make sure the villain got what he deserved. This guy was just soo slippery that I wished we knew for certain that he paid for all his crimes.<br /><br />Victor Slezak kicked ass with the narration. He has that tough guy voice that's just perfect for Sandra Brown's heroes.<br /><br />Overall, an excellent book which I recommend to all lovers of romantic suspense.</span>
  <a data-text-id="1554779675138911874" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_123376707" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/123376707" />
    <a title="Jane Stewart" class="left imgcol" href="/user/show/3789528-jane-stewart"><img alt="Jane Stewart" src="https://images.gr-assets.com/users/1346001994p2/3789528.jpg" /></a>

  <div class="left bodycol">
    <div class="reviewHeader uitext stacked">
        <a class="reviewDate createdAt right" href="/review/show/123376707?book_show_action=true">Sep 25, 2010</a>

      <span itemprop="author" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Person">
        <a title="Jane Stewart" class="user" itemprop="url" name="Jane Stewart" href="/user/show/3789528-jane-stewart">Jane Stewart</a>
      </span>

        rated it
        <span class=" staticStars notranslate" title="it was amazing"><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10">it was amazing</span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span><span size="15x15" class="staticStar p10"></span></span>

          <span class="greyText">&nbsp;&middot;&nbsp;</span>
          <a class="lightGreyText" title="Mass Market Paperback 9780446611800" href="/book/show/790250.Envy">review of another edition</a>


        

          <div class="uitext greyText bookshelves">
            Shelves:
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3789528-jane-stewart?shelf=romantic-suspense">romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3789528-jane-stewart?shelf=5-star-romantic-suspense">5-star-romantic-suspense</a>, 
              <a class="actionLinkLite" href="/review/list/3789528-jane-stewart?shelf=mystery-suspense-thriller-romance">mystery-suspense-thriller-romance</a>
          </div>
    </div>


        <div class="reviewText stacked">
              <span id="reviewTextContainer123376707" class="readable"
              >
            
<span id="freeTextContainer499542654857201788">Frighteningly evil bad guy, and interesting romantic development.<br/><br/>I read this nine years ago and gave it 4 stars. I recently bought the audiobook and changed my opinion. It’s a definite 5 stars. Nine years ago I guess I wanted more emotional draw. But now I think it’s great just the way it is.<br/><br/>Victor Slezak narrated the audiobook. He is excellent.<br/><br/>My original review from nine years ago follows.<br/><br/>STORY BRIEF:<br/>Two stories are being told. The first story is about Maris, an editor and executive in her fat</span>
  <span id="freeText499542654857201788" style="display:none">Frighteningly evil bad guy, and interesting romantic development.<br /><br />I read this nine years ago and gave it 4 stars. I recently bought the audiobook and changed my opinion. It’s a definite 5 stars. Nine years ago I guess I wanted more emotional draw. But now I think it’s great just the way it is.<br /><br />Victor Slezak narrated the audiobook. He is excellent.<br /><br />My original review from nine years ago follows.<br /><br />STORY BRIEF:<br />Two stories are being told. The first story is about Maris, an editor and executive in her father’s publishing company Matherly Press. Noah was a famous author who came to work at Matherly Press. He and Maris married. Maris recently read an unsolicited manuscript in her slush pile. It was a prologue titled “Envy” submitted by P.M.E. with no phone and no address. She loved it and eventually finds the author (Parker Evans) living on an island off Georgia. She travels there to discuss the book. She ends up staying longer than she planned.<br /><br />The second story is “Envy” (the novel Parker is writing). “Envy” starts with Todd, Roark and a girl renting a boat. They had been drinking. Something happens and the boat returns with only Todd on it. The story then goes back in time showing Todd and Roark before the boating accident. They had been college roommates and aspiring authors.<br /><br />REVIEWER’S OPINION:<br />Very good. Solid writing. None of my pet peeves. It’s an in depth mystery with some nice romantic development. After I had been reading for over an hour, I was so worried about what would happen to the good guys that I had to read the ending before going back to finish the story. Then I was able to relax a little more and enjoy it. The bad guy was frighteningly evil and deceptive. Mystery lovers should love it. To get 5 stars from me I would have wanted a little more wow factor or emotional draw. This was more of an intellectual draw, but very, very good. The sex scenes were a little weak on passion/emotion, but should appeal to romance lovers. Mystery/thriller lovers might not want the sex scenes.<br /><br />I noticed other reviewers saying there is not much mystery because one can guess a key plot point early on. I too guessed this, but other mysteries remained about what the main characters were going to do and how they were going to do it. I was fine with the mystery.<br /><br />DATA:<br />Narrative mode: 3rd person. Story length: 549 pages. Swearing language: strong, including religious words. Sexual language: strong. Number of sex scenes: 6. Total number of sex scene pages: 15. Setting: 1985 – 2002 Manhattan, NY, St. Anne Island, Georgia, Key West, Florida, and Tennessee. Copyright: 2001. Genre: romantic suspense, mystery suspense thriller.<br /></span>
  <a data-text-id="499542654857201788" href="#" onclick="swapContent($(this));; return false;">...more</a>

          </span>
        </div>

<div id="review_139666822" class="review" itemprop="reviews" itemscope itemtype="http://schema.org/Review">
  <link itemprop="url" href="https://www.goodreads.com/review/show/139666822" />
